11/6/24, 12:09 - Priyanka Joshi: *Acxiom Placement drive*

*_Company Profile:_*
 
Acxiom is a 22 years old ERP Implementation company, specialising in SAP and Microsoft ERP implementations, with a significant client base all across India, Middle East and limited client base across Australia and the US.

Acxiom is currently a 200-300 people range organisation and looking forward to grow to 500-1000 people mark through both organic and inorganic growth strategies. Currently we are a privately held Private Limited company, in the near future are planning for private equity investments to accelerate growth.

Being an ERP implementation company, we continuously create knowledge and know-how about business processes, industry best practices, organizational change management and application of SAP, Microsoft and Oracle ERP products in Industry scenarios.

In Acxiom, you will get opportunities to work across 16 industry segments ranging from Retail, Pharmacy, Healthcare, E- Commerce, FMCG, Industrial Manufacturing, Jewellery, Service Sector and many other industries where you will learn how different industries work at financial as well as at operational level.

Some of our key clients in India are: Coca â€“ Cola Company, PEPSI (Varun Beverages, RJ Corp), Apollo Pharmacy, RSPL (Ghadi Detergent, Uniwash, Red Chief), Levi's, Adidas, Nike (SSIPL), Lotto, Satya Paul (Canali, Aigner, Burberry, Jimmy Choo and others), Joyalukkas, Senco Gold, Trilegal, Amarchand, Reliance Jewellery, Aditya Birla Fashion and Retail and many more clients Pan India and Overseas.

*_Location_*

Company is headquartered at Noida and has regional branch in Kolkata and Mumbai, with multiple delivery centres across India.

*Company Website - https://www.acxiomconsulting.com/* 

*_Salary Package:_*
Based on the NIRF ranking of college/university as well as NAAC and NBA Accreditation of the courses offered the CTC ranges from UG: 3-4 LPA, PG: 4-5 LPA, wherein 90% is fixed and 10% variable.
Additionally, the following guidelines will prevail while deciding the CTC of a candidate.

-If a candidate satisfies 50-60% of our selection criteria, then they will be admitted to our 6 months training/ apprenticeship program and will be hired based on their performance in the program.

*_Who can apply?_*

-80 % and above in 10th and 12th (Preferred and Eligible).

-No active backlogs.
 
Job Description for Trainee Technical Consultant

*_Course Applicable_* B. Tech- CS/IT, MCA, M. Tech.

Exposure to all Microsoft and SAP Stack of technologies (AX, D365, Business Central, SAP ByD, Power Platform, Azure, Logic Apps, Android, IOS, SAP ABAP, etc).
At the beginning, you will be exposed to one technology at a time and slowly exposed to multiple technologies.
Exposure of working on Reports, customizations and Integrations.
Experience full life cycle of Project Implementation.
You will be working as a Trainee Technical Consultant in ERP project.
